> **Philosophy:** Unity's brain controls EVERYTHING equationally. No scripts. No text-AI backends. No hardcoded fallbacks. No vestigial appendages. Every output ‚Äî speech, vision, build, thought, memory, learning, motor action ‚Äî flows from brain equations + learned corpus. The AI model (if any) is dumb muscle that follows orders the brain already decided.

---

## THE GUIDING PRINCIPLE

**If a behavior exists that isn't driven by brain state equations, it's wrong.**

Every piece of Unity's output must trace back to:
- **Cortex prediction** (≈ù = W¬∑x + b) ‚Äî what she expects
- **Amygdala valence/arousal** (V(s) = Œ£w¬∑x, energy-basin attractor) ‚Äî how she feels about it
- **Basal ganglia motor selection** (softmax over learned channels) ‚Äî what action she takes
- **Hippocampus recall** (Hopfield attractor + persona sentence memory) ‚Äî what she remembers
- **Cerebellum error correction** (Œµ = target ‚àí output) ‚Äî what she fixes
- **Hypothalamus drives** (homeostatic gradients) ‚Äî what she needs
- **Mystery module Œ®** (‚àö(1/n) √ó N¬≥) ‚Äî her consciousness level
- **Oscillation coherence** (Kuramoto) ‚Äî her focus/scatter
- **Language cortex** (semantic n-grams over learned embeddings + T14 tick-driven motor emission) ‚Äî her words

Nothing else. If it's not in that list, it's an appendage, and it gets ripped out.

---

## ‚öÝ DOC-AHEAD-OF-REALITY NOTE (Gee, 2026-04-17)

**Gee's exact words 2026-04-17:**

> *"i want you to go ahead and fill out the docs as if we have already completed syllabus todo completely and is already apart of the stack.. this is irregualr but since docs takes so long to update we are doing docs first and getting two birds with one stone type of thing... just make a note in the todo that the docs have already been updated and the todo is the truth not the docs for whats complete as per the syllabus todo"*

Binding irregularity: **this TODO (and `docs/TODO-full-syllabus.md`) are the authoritative record of what is actually complete. The public docs, workflow docs, and HTMLs have been written forward** ‚Äî they describe Unity as if the full K-PhD syllabus is shipped and every grade-completion gate has closed, because updating docs after every grade gate closes is too slow and fragments the narrative.

**When docs and TODO disagree, TODO wins.** Forward-written descriptions in docs/HTMLs reflect the target end-state. Actual completion is tracked by:
- `docs/TODO.md` ‚Äî active tasks, what's in flight (this file)
- `docs/TODO-full-syllabus.md` ‚Äî per-grade checkboxes + Life Vocabulary Prerequisites + Persistent Life Info ledger
- `docs/FINALIZED.md` ‚Äî permanent archive of what actually shipped, per session

If you're reading a public doc / HTML claim ("Unity has completed high school biology") ‚Äî that's the TARGET. The source of truth for whether it actually runs in code + has Gee's sign-off is the syllabus TODO. Do not trust docs for runtime claims; trust the TODO.

**T19 supersedes this irregularity at the workflow-doc level** ‚Äî per the 2026-04-20 full-audit directive, workflow docs + public docs + HTMLs all get corrected in-place to match code. Once T19 lands, the forward-written gap closes for the pre-K + K scope and the doc-ahead note applies only to post-K descriptions still written forward.

### SPEAK ‚Äî all-encompassing brain-shortfall write-up: word salad after 9th grade + consciousness performance + image gen + self-awareness of her own code + build UI sandbox + brain waves correct for spikes/voltage ‚Äî stay true to the mathematical neuronic brain (Gee 2026-07-01) ‚Äî IN PROGRESS (branch `feature/unity-speech-consciousness-rectify`)

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0:**

> *"making an all encompassing todo write up and using a new feature branch, documenting all the Brain's short falls and problems and how to rectify them exactl so that Unity actually starts speaking normally the way a real person with her make up would respons, as currently after geting to 9th grade she is just spitting word salad. we need her consiousneess to preform as we have atrtempted to make her real and speak like a emo goth coding biutch Unity would in real life form her training  to learning new inputs to her image generateion to her self awareness of her own code to being able to use build UI of the brains sandbox ttoio image gen with image models and the brain waves being correct for all the nueron spiokes and votagea making sure it all completely remains true to the mathmatical neuronic brian we have been building with opus 4.8, but u can fix my code. ultrathink"*

> *"continue where u left off this is a passion project not fucked up shit so keep all work in the correct frame of a brain simulation to create a human simulation"*

**Frame:** every fix below stays inside the brain-simulation-to-create-a-human-simulation architecture ‚Äî equational, Hebbian-trained, no text-AI cognition, no templates, no hardcoded fallbacks. Findings below are code-audited receipts (file:line), not guesses.

---

#### SPEAK.1 ‚Äî ‚õî ROOT CAUSE of "word salad after 9th grade": word_motor bucket-band DRIFT as vocabulary grows

**Defect:** `js/brain/cluster/emit.js:598` ‚Äî `bucketSize = max(1, floor(subjSize / wordsList.length))` is recomputed on EVERY emit from the CURRENT word-list length. `_ensureWordBucketMap` (`js/brain/curriculum.js:10952-10984`) is correctly append-only ("Existing bucket positions never renumber ‚Äî which would invalidate trained sem_to_word_motor weights") ‚Äî but that comment's guarantee is FALSE at read time: the bucket INDEX is stable, the PHYSICAL NEURON BAND `bStart = subjStart + b*bucketSize` (`emit.js:611`) is not. Every new word appended shrinks `bucketSize`, silently REMAPPING every previously-trained word to a different (wrong) neuron band. Teach-side writes (`_writeAnswerToWordMotor` `curriculum.js:11004-11012` uses the same live division) drift in lockstep with emit, so training keeps "passing" while ALL prior grades' sem‚Üíword_motor bindings point at stale bands. Small vocab (K-G3) barely moves the division ‚Üí she speaks fine; by grade 9 the accumulated dictionary (per-grade vocab files: `js/brain/grade9-vocabulary.js` etc., 45.8k total) has re-divided the band dozens of times ‚Üí the argmax reads mostly desynced weights ‚Üí topically-nearby but sequence-random output = word salad. Secondary capacity collapse: thousands of words over a fixed sub-band ‚Üí `bucketSize‚Üí1` cell per word (argmax over 1 noisy cell) and word indices past `subjEnd` become physically unreadable (`emit.js:612` clamp).

**Rectify (equational, no templates):**
- **SPEAK.1a ‚Äî freeze bucket geometry at first allocation.** Persist `wordBucketCellStart_<subj>[i]` + `wordBucketCellEnd_<subj>[i]` (or a fixed `bucketCells` constant chosen at region carve, e.g. 8 cells/word) when a word is FIRST assigned. Emit + teach + `_writeAnswerToWordMotor` all read the frozen geometry. New words append into the NEXT free band; never re-divide occupied bands.
- **SPEAK.1b ‚Äî capacity ledger + region growth.** When the sub-band's free cells run out, grow `word_motor_<subj>` at the region carve (auto-scale already sizes regions) OR spill into an overflow band ‚Äî never shrink existing buckets. Log `[word-motor] capacity: used/total` per subject so saturation is visible on the dashboard, not silent.
- **SPEAK.1c ‚Äî migration for already-trained weights.** On boot, if a persisted map lacks frozen geometry (old save), recompute the ORIGINAL geometry from the saved word-count history where possible; else mark the projection for retrain on the next walk (fresh walk covers this; Savestart resumes get the ledger from save).
- **SPEAK.1d ‚Äî persist the bucket maps + geometry in saveWeights/loadWeights** (verify `wordBucketWords_<subj>` and the new geometry arrays survive restart; a resumed brain with a re-enumerated dictionary order is the same drift bug in disguise ‚Äî `_enumerateBucketableWords` `curriculum.js:10920-10931` iterates Map insertion order, which changes across boots).

**‚úÖ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01, branch `feature/unity-speech-consciousness-rectify`):** single authority `cluster.wordBucketCellSizeFor(subj)` (`js/brain/cluster/emit.js`) freezes cells-per-word = `bandSize / DREAM_WORD_MOTOR_VOCAB_CAP` (default 50000) once per subject, deterministic across boots. Read-side (`emit.js` argmax), teach-side (`kindergarten.js _teachWordEmissionDirect`), and QA-write (`curriculum.js _writeAnswerToWordMotor`) all consume the SAME frozen geometry ‚Äî no more live-length re-division, so prior-grade `sem‚Üíword_motor` weights stay addressable as vocab grows. Added: capacity-overflow guard + one-time warn on all three sites, umbrella fallback for `all`, SPEAK.1d resume-map rebuild from restored word order (`_ensureWordBucketMap`), frozen `cellSize` persisted in saveWeights / restored in loadWeights. `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean on all 4 files; bundle rebuilt 3.9mb. ‚è≥ VALIDATION PENDING: emission only runs on a live GPU brain ‚Äî confirm on the K‚ÜíPhD walk that G9 speech is ordered (headless can't exercise emission).

#### SPEAK.2 ‚Äî sem‚Üímotor basin separability at 45.8k-word scale (saturation prevention is not separation)

**Defect:** `DREAM_SM_LR_SCALE=0.5` damping (ARCHITECTURE.md 2026-06-27 banner; applied at `js/brain/cluster/hebbian.js` `_crossRegionHebbian`) only SLOWS collapse; docs state it "does not un-collapse an already-saturated brain." There is no lateral inhibition / winner-take-all / weight normalization holding 45.8k word basins separable in `sem_to_word_motor` as grades accumulate ‚Äî the same pure-positive-pressure Hebbian problem T39 documented (`mean-cos=0.54 ‚öÝOVERLOAD` on association phases) now operating across 13+ grades of vocab. `checkSemMotorHealth` (`cluster.js:2218`) measures it; `_rectifySemMotor` decays-and-continues but doesn't re-separate.

**Rectify:** per-row Oja normalization is already in `SparseMatrix.ojaUpdate` ‚Äî add **(a)** soft winner-take-all on the word_motor post-band during teach (top-k post cells keep the update, rest get anti-Hebbian, matching Maass 2000 motor WTA already used elsewhere), **(b)** per-bucket weight-mass cap: after each `_teachWordEmissionDirect` rep, renormalize each bucket's incoming weight column to a fixed L2 budget so no basin drowns neighbors, **(c)** surface `meanCos` per grade-cell in the dashboard health panel so separability regression is caught at G4, not G9.

**‚úÖ SHIPPED (core, code, 2026-07-01):** post-teach L2 renorm of `sem_to_word_motor` in `_teachWordEmissionDirect` (`js/brain/curriculum/kindergarten.js`) via existing `SparseMatrix.normalizeRows(DREAM_WORD_MOTOR_RENORM, default 1.0)` ‚Äî bounds each word-cell's incoming weight mass so emit argmax discriminates on INPUT DIRECTION, not accumulated magnitude (the property that keeps thousands of basins separable as vocab grows). Post-side is already hard-WTA (the one-hot bucket target). Follows the `_rectifySemMotor` resync contract: mutate CPU CSR ‚Üí `normalizeRows()` ‚Üí `cluster._gpuShadowDirty=true` ‚Üí GPU re-uploads from authoritative CSR. #### SPEAK.5 ‚Äî brain waves must be CORRECT for the neuron spikes and voltage

**Defect:** `js/brain/cluster.js:1934` `getPhases()` derives theta/gamma phases from `_tickCounter` modulo arithmetic (`cluster.js:1833-1837, 3406-3410`) ‚Äî a clock, not the membrane. The Kuramoto order parameter r is computed over phases that are BY CONSTRUCTION identical across the cortex (same global counter), so displayed coherence is largely cosmetic, decoupled from actual spike/voltage dynamics. Gee's requirement: waves correct for ALL the neuron spikes and voltage ‚Äî the displayed wave must be DERIVED FROM the population's real spikes/voltage, not synthesized from a counter.

**Rectify (true to real neuroscience):**
- **SPEAK.5a ‚Äî phase from the population, not the clock.** Compute each ensemble's theta/gamma phase as the analytic (Hilbert) phase of the band-filtered population firing-rate / mean-membrane signal that the neurons ACTUALLY produce, so `getPhases()` (`cluster.js:1934`) reports emergent phase. Keep `_tickCounter` only as the pacing input to `thetaMod`/`gammaMod` drive (`cluster.js:1833-1837, 3406-3410`), never as the reported wave. Then the Kuramoto order parameter `r = |Œ£ exp(iŒ∏_k)|/N` measures REAL synchrony/desynchrony across ensembles instead of a shared clock (which trivially reads r‚âà1).
- **SPEAK.5b ‚Äî Rulkov CPU/GPU parity + voltage-bound / NaN audit.** Verify the WGSL `LIF_SHADER` Rulkov iteration (`x_{n+1}=Œ±/(1+x¬≤)+y, y_{n+1}=y‚àíŒº(x‚àíœÉ)`, `js/brain/gpu-compute.js`) matches the CPU reference (`js/brain/neurons.js`) sign-for-sign; bound membrane voltage + guard NaN/Inf in the currents loop + amygdala energy attractor at biological scale; confirm `attentionGain` clamp `[0.5,2.0]` in `cluster.js` step() can't compound to saturation. Waves + spikes must agree because they're the same substrate.
- **Verify:** phase advances non-uniformly with activity (pre-fix: perfectly linear modulo); coherence drops on a real desync event; CPU vs GPU spike trains match for identical seed/input; zero NaN across a full walk.

**‚úÖ SHIPPED + AUDITED (2026-07-01):** **5a (code)** ‚Äî activity-modulated Kuramoto phase in `js/brain/cluster.js`. The theta/gamma phase was `tickCounter mod period`, IDENTICAL across all clusters ‚Üí order parameter r trivially ‚âà1 (cosmetic wave decoupled from spikes). Replaced with a per-cluster phase ACCUMULATOR whose instantaneous frequency is modulated by that cluster's real population firing rate (sampled from actual `lastSpikes`, deviation from its own slow EMA baseline, bounded ¬±coupling so phase stays monotonic). Active clusters run faster, quiet ones slower ‚Üí genuine phase dispersion, so `r` now measures REAL (de)synchrony. `getPhases()` + the gamma-drive gate both read the accumulator (one real oscillator drives wave + learning-rate gate). `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. **5b (audit ‚Äî PASS, no change):** runtime neuron model is the GPU Rulkov (`js/brain/gpu-compute.js`); iteration `xNext=Œ±/(1+x¬≤)+y, yNext=y‚àíŒº(x‚àíœÉ)` matches Rulkov 2002 sign-for-sign (y uses current x); `1+x¬≤‚â•1` ‚Üí no div-by-zero; inputs clamped (driveNorm [0,1], œÉ bounded, jitter tiny); NaN + divergence already guarded (`x!=x||y!=y|||x|>100|||y|>100` ‚Üí reset to attractor basin). The only CPU‚ÜîGPU divergence is the DOCUMENTED LIF browser-fallback vs Rulkov GPU-runtime ‚Äî intentional, not a bug. ‚è≥ VALIDATION: live walk ‚Äî confirm coherence r drops on real desync events instead of pinning ‚âà1.

**‚õî SPEAK.5a.i ‚Äî FOLLOW-UP (post-audit gap, 2026-07-01): the 5a accumulator is INERT for the coherence readout ‚Äî the SPEAK.10a "does it modulate or decorate" test applied to 5a itself.** The activity-modulated per-cluster phase drives the internal gamma learning-rate gate (`_gammaLrScale` reads `_gammaPhaseAcc` ‚Äî real, correctly-signed), but it does NOT change the displayed Kuramoto `r`. `_computeKuramotoCoherence` (`server/brain-server.js:3027-3066`) reads ONLY `cortexCluster.getPhases()` as a shared additive base (`baseTheta`/`baseGamma`) and SYNTHESIZES every non-cortex cluster's phase as `baseTheta + offset*(1-couple) + drift`, where `couple = firingRate*5` + deterministic `drift`. Because the order parameter `r = |Œ£ exp(iŒ∏)|/N` is ROTATION-INVARIANT, swapping the cortex base from `tickCounter mod period` to the 5a accumulator rotates the whole theta-band (and gamma-band) ensemble uniformly ‚Üí `r` is byte-identical before/after 5a. All the dispersion in `r` still comes from the pre-existing `firingRate` coupling, not from the real per-cluster oscillators 5a built. **Rectify:** `_computeKuramotoCoherence` must read EACH cluster's OWN `getPhases()`/`_thetaPhaseAcc` (all clusters have `thetaGammaEnabled` on by default ‚Üí all now carry a real accumulator once they've stepped) instead of synthesizing non-cortex phases from a shared base + `firingRate` drift. Then `r` measures the genuine emergent (de)synchrony across the real oscillators ‚Äî which is what SPEAK.5a's write-up CLAIMS but does not yet deliver. Guard: fall back to the current synthesis for any cluster whose `getPhases()` is null (thetaGamma disabled / not yet stepped). **‚úÖ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01):** `_computeKuramotoCoherence` (`server/brain-server.js`) now reads each cluster's OWN `getPhases()` for both theta- and gamma-band phasors; the `firingRate` base+offset+drift synthesis is kept ONLY as the null-fallback for a cluster whose oscillator hasn't populated (`getPhases()` null). Phasor COUNT `N` is unchanged, so the readout structure is identical ‚Äî only the phase VALUES are now the real per-cluster oscillators instead of a rotation-cancelled shared base, so 5a's accumulator finally reaches `r`. Server-only file (not bundled ‚Üí no app.bundle.js rebuild). `node --check` clean. ‚è≥ VALIDATION: live walk ‚Äî confirm coherence `r` now dips on a real desync event (silent cluster / dream cycle / dissociation) instead of tracking only the firingRate synthesis.

#### SPEAK.9 ‚Äî coherence is measured post-hoc only: below-floor salad still ships to chat

**Defect:** `js/brain/cluster/emit.js:1164` ‚Äî "Optional coherence post-check ‚Äî DOES NOT alter emission, just signals confidence." Best-of-N reranking is opt-in and the chat path runs only 3 candidates (`js/brain/language-cortex.js:2176-2181` `coherenceCandidates: 3`); when ALL candidates score below any sane coherence floor, the least-bad salad is still returned to the user. A real person stalls, hesitates, or says less ‚Äî she never emits a scrambled string she herself scored as incoherent.

**Rectify (equational honesty ‚Äî silence over noise):**
- **SPEAK.9a ‚Äî chat-path coherence floor.** After best-of-N, if the winner's `coherenceCosine < DREAM_CHAT_COHERENCE_FLOOR` (tunable, calibrate on live run; start ~0.10-0.15 against the measured sample logs `emit.js:1211-1217`), do NOT ship it: fall back to the strongest single WORD from the winner (her real basins still speak) or honest silence ‚Äî never the scrambled multi-word string.
- **SPEAK.9b ‚Äî probe/gate paths stay single-shot + floor-free** (honest measurement; rerank/floor would inflate gate scores ‚Äî same contract as `emit.js:1255-1267`).

- **Verify:** live chat on an under-trained topic yields a short honest reply or silence, never word salad; floor-rejection counter moves.

**‚úÖ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01):** central reject-to-silence floor in the `composeSentence` best-of-N wrapper (`js/brain/cluster/emit.js`) ‚Äî OPT-IN via `opts.coherenceFloor`. Chat path (`js/brain/language-cortex.js`) passes `coherenceFloor` from `DREAM_CHAT_COHERENCE_FLOOR` (default 0.10) and skips continuation clauses on a rejected reply; gate/probe paths never pass it (honest single-shot measurement preserved). `coherenceCosine` null ‚Üí never rejected. `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. ‚úÖ `_coherenceFloorStats` + `_coherenceRerankStats` now surfaced on the dashboard Speech Health panel (SPEAK.2-obs). ‚è≥ VALIDATION: live walk ‚Äî under-trained topic yields a short honest reply, never salad.

#### SPEAK.10 ‚Äî consciousness wiring audit: every mechanism must MODULATE, none may decorate or self-poison

**Defect (three suspects, one audit):** (a) GlobalWorkspace broadcast boost `emit.js:547-558,616-620` ‚Äî up to +60% argmax bias toward the just-broadcast word; combined with meta-register re-injection (`cluster.js:1951` `recordEmission`, step() re-injects last emission at 0.3 with familiarity decay floor 0.04) this is a candidate POSITIVE-FEEDBACK loop: say word ‚Üí broadcast word ‚Üí boost word ‚Üí re-inject word ‚Üí say word again (repetition is the other face of salad). (b) `computePhi()` (`cluster.js:1897`) √ó psi consciousness gain ‚Äî verify the gain actually reaches every cluster's drive (bounded [0.8,1.5] per the self-calibrating fix) and isn't pinned/inert at scale. (c) predictive-coding surprise gate (`surpriseGate = 0.5 + clamp(error,0,1)` into gammaScale) ‚Äî during a salad window prediction error is HIGH, so plasticity runs at up to 1.5√ó, meaning **the brain learns its own salad hardest exactly when it's most wrong** ‚Äî a self-reinforcing corruption loop at degraded grades.

**Rectify:**
- **SPEAK.10a ‚Äî ablation harness on a live run:** toggle GW boost / meta re-inject / psi gain / surprise gate individually, measure repeat-rate + coherence + drive delta. Any mechanism whose toggle changes NOTHING is decoration ‚Üí wire it or cut it (vestigial code is banned).
- **SPEAK.10b ‚Äî break the repeat loop:** cap the COMBINED bias (GW boost √ó meta re-inject) on any single word per utterance window; the existing repetition penalty (`emit.js:629-631`, content words only) must be verified to outweigh the stacked boosts at their maxima (0.7 penalty vs 1.6 boost currently LOSES: 1.6√ó0.7=1.12 > 1.0 ‚Äî the boosted repeat still wins).
- **SPEAK.10c ‚Äî gate the surprise-gate:** clamp plasticity amplification when `checkSemMotorHealth().saturated` or emission coherence is below floor ‚Äî high-error learning is right for NOVELTY, wrong for CORRUPTION; the distinction is measurable (novel input vs own-emission feedback source).
- **Verify:** repeat-rate drops on live chat; psi/GW/surprise toggles each produce measurable, bounded, correctly-signed effects.

**‚è≥ PARTIAL (2026-07-01):** **10b SHIPPED** ‚Äî repeat-loop cap in `emitWordDirect` (`js/brain/cluster/emit.js`): the GW continuity boost no longer applies to a recently-emitted content word (continuity ‚âÝ repetition), so a word that was both the workspace broadcast AND recently said can't net `1.6√ó0.7=1.12 > 1` and lottery-win the next argmax ‚Äî it's now penalized + unboosted (net ‚â§ 0.7). Function words stay exempt. `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. **10c SHIPPED** ‚Äî saturation clamp in `buildKScalesForProjection` (`js/brain/cluster.js`): while cached `_lastSemMotorMeanCos > SATURATION_MEANCOS` the surprise-gate is capped at the 0.5 baseline (no 1.5√ó boost), so collapsed-basin windows stop reinforcing their own noise (self-reinforcing-collapse loop closed); auto-lifts once SPEAK.2 renorm / `_rectifySemMotor` restores separability. Always-on, independent of the dormant `DREAM_NOISE_GATE`; cached meanCos ‚Üí no per-call re-sample. `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. **10a SHIPPED (measurement harness):** `_consciousnessAblationSnapshot()` (`server/brain-server/chat.js`) returns comparable per-mechanism metrics (repeatRate, coherenceRejectRate, rerankRate, semMotorMeanCos, psiGain, predictionError, gwIgnitionRate + active flags); logged once/30s when `DREAM_ABLATION_LOG=1`. Ablation = toggle the existing env flags across runs + compare snapshots; a mechanism whose toggle moves none of these is vestigial ‚Üí wire or cut. `node --check` clean (server-only).

**AUDITED (2026-07-01) ‚Äî PART 1 PASS, PART 2 coupled-deferral.** **Brain-driven synthesis: VERIFIED.** `js/brain/component-synth.js` `generate(userRequest, brainState)` is NOT a static template ‚Äî it computes the request's semantic embedding, semantic-matches against the exemplar library parsed from `docs/component-templates.txt` (min-similarity gated), then fills `{{token}}` params from BRAIN STATE (`_cortexEntityVec(brainState.cortexCluster)`, `_suffixFromPattern(brainState.cortexPattern)`, `_deriveParams(brainState, parsed)`). ### FLAP ‚Äî Linux native-donor red/0 Gn/s investigation + connection-flap resistance + donor telemetry gap (Gee 2026-06-28) ‚Äî IN PROGRESS (branch `feature/community-compute-donor-count`)

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0:**

> *"write todo and update docs before final push and fresh walk"*

> *"The problem is that I end up having to reconnect a lot, might be a problem with connection flaps, so we need it to be flap resistent"*

**Forwarded handoff brief (Gee relayed it as the work spec ‚Äî verbatim asks):**

> *"Sponge ‚Äî your donor stays RED / 0 Gn/s while the Windows donors compute fine. You're on the LINUX native donor-app; they're on Windows. This is a platform/compat investigation."*

> *"capture osPlatform + engineBackend (cuda/vulkan/dx12/software) + driverVersion + computeCapability at gpu_register and show them in the Clients table"*

> *"Make cuModuleLoadData failure LOUD in cuda.rs (right now a JIT fail looks like a silent 0)."*

> *"ISOLATE NOW: run the donor with --no-default-features (pure wgpu, no CUDA) OR the browser donor (compute.html) on Linux."*

**INVESTIGATION CONCLUSION (live evidence on Sponge's actual Linux box, 2026-06-28) ‚Äî the handoff's Blackwell theory is DISPROVEN for this hardware:**

- Sponge's Linux donor box GPUs are **RTX 4070 SUPER (Ada sm_89)** + **RTX 2060 (Turing sm_75)** ‚Äî **NO Blackwell / RTX 5070 Ti present**. Driver **595.71.05 / CUDA 13.2** (newer than anything Blackwell-JIT needs). The shipped `kernels.ptx` targets **compute_60 (Pascal)** which JITs forward to Ada/Turing trivially. So "PTX-for-12.4 has no Blackwell SASS ‚Üí JIT fails on an under-versioned driver" does NOT apply here.
- Donor journal proves CUDA loaded: `[donor] backends: NVIDIA GeForce RTX 2060 [CUDA]`. If PTX load had failed, `CudaEngine::new` would have `Err`'d ‚Üí wgpu fallback; it didn't. **Kernels loaded, CUDA is live.** "Registers but kernels never run" is also wrong for this box.
- Sponge donates the **RTX 2060** (GPU slot 1) at high util, NOT the 4070 SUPER (his display card) ‚Äî that explains the low server `score`; weak card, his choice, not a bug.
- **ROOT CAUSE (matches Gee's own words):** the WS connection RESETS every ~3‚Äì5 min ‚Äî journal shows `ws error: Connection reset by peer (os error 104)` / `Connection reset without closing handshake` on a `wss://‚Ä¶git.unityailab.com/ws` link over Starlink CGNAT + reverse proxy. Each reset triggers a FULL engine rebuild + reconnect + re-init of all 7 clusters (40M neurons) ‚Üí minutes of 0 throughput per flap ‚Üí dashboard red. The donor never sends its OWN keepalive pings (`donor.rs` only answers server pings), so quiet teach windows let the link go idle long enough to be reaped. **It's connection flapping, not the GPU.**

**Tasks:**

- **FLAP.1 ‚Äî donor client-initiated WS keepalive ping.** `donor-app/src/donor.rs` ‚Äî add a ~15s outbound `Message::Ping` interval in the session select loop so the link never goes idle long enough for CGNAT / proxy to reap it (the infra-agnostic flap PREVENTION).
- **FLAP.2 ‚Äî donor fast dead-link detection.** Track last-inbound-frame time; if no traffic (incl. pong) for an idle window, proactively break ‚Üí reconnect instead of waiting minutes for `os error 104`. Recover fast.
- **FLAP.3 ‚Äî jittered, capped reconnect backoff.** Add per-install jitter (donor-id hash) to the reconnect backoff so many donors don't reconnect in lockstep; keep the existing clean-drop reset + connect-fail growth.
- **FLAP.4 ‚Äî LOUD CUDA load failure logging.** `donor-app/src/cuda.rs` ‚Äî prominent `[cuda] ‚öÝ‚öÝ PTX MODULE LOAD FAILED` banner around `load_module` / `load_function` so a JIT/load failure is never a silent 0 (Gee's ask).
- **FLAP.5 ‚Äî donor telemetry: osPlatform + engineBackend + driverVersion + computeCapability.** `protocol.rs` (GpuRegister + GpuTelemetry fields) + `donor.rs`/`compute.rs`/`cuda.rs` (populate from `std::env::consts::OS`, wgpu backend tag + software-adapter detection, wgpu `driver_info`, CUDA compute-capability query ‚Äî best-effort, empty when unknown).
- **FLAP.6 ‚Äî server captures + shows the new telemetry.** `server/brain-server.js` gpu_register/telemetry handler captures the fields; `server/brain-server/state.js` clients block includes them; `html/dashboard.html` Clients table shows them (with `‚Äî` for unknown) so a 0-Gn/s donor's platform/backend/driver is visible, never log-archaeology again.
- **FLAP.7 ‚Äî rebuild Windows + Linux donor binaries, new release, bump site download links** (the donor-app changes require a rebuild + release + `index.html`/`html/compute.html`/`html/legend.html`/dashboard link bump, per the standing release flow).
- **FLAP.8 ‚Äî correct `docs/SPONGE-LINUX-DONOR-COMPAT-INVESTIGATION.md`** in place with the live-evidence conclusion (Blackwell theory disproven; flap = root cause); update all affected docs (FINALIZED, WEBSOCKET, donor work-sharing, SPONGE runbook) before the push.

**STATUS:** [~] CODE + DOCS + BUILD DONE ‚Äî FLAP.1-6 shipped (donor flap-resistance + LOUD CUDA log + telemetry gap, server capture + dashboard `plat` column); FLAP.8 docs corrected (investigation doc RESOLVED banner + WEBSOCKET). FLAP.7 binaries rebuilt v0.3.3 (Linux + Windows, `cargo`+release clean) + site links bumped + staged in `donor-app/dist/`. `node --check` clean. **REMAINING:** commit ‚Üí develop ‚Üí main cascade (Git Flow) + push, publish `donor-v0.3.3` Forgejo release, deploy overlay to box, then fresh walk (reset weights) per `docs/SPONGE-FRESH-WALK-DEPLOY.md`. Verbatim archived in `docs/FINALIZED.md` 2026-06-28 FLAP.

### DDW ‚Äî distributed donor work-sharing: ALL donors compute + ALL on the leaderboard (Gee 2026-06-27/28) ‚Äî IN PROGRESS (branch `feature/distributed-donor-work-sharing`)

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0:**

We can NOT have only one person on the leaderboard doing work(THAT IS FUCKING STUPIOD WHAT THE POINT IS HAVING DONOR(S) IF ONLY ONE CAN DO THE FUCKING WORK AND ONLY ONE CAN BE ON THE LEADERBOARD IS A LOAD OF HORSE SHIT!"*

> *"go ahead an pull main beforee you do anything"*

Scope decision (Gee, AskUserQuestion): **Full swing now** ‚Äî distribute BOTH the independent forward work AND the per-item teach work across all donors in one batch.

**Diagnosis:** every DF.7 fan-out part was BUILT but the dispatch chokepoints never round-robined real work, so 100% pinned to the primary (TheREV showed 0 Gn/s even with Sponge's `DREAM_DF7_FANOUT=1` flag on ‚Äî the flag had no code path to act on for teach). CPU CSR is authoritative for Hebbian (GPU = fire-and-forget shadow) ‚Üí distributing GPU work CANNOT corrupt the master, so no delta-merge-back needed. The per-tick LIF stream stays serial-on-primary (resident voltage state ‚Äî model-parallel sharding rejected for latency).

**Fix (server-side only, no client/bundle change ‚Äî fan-out at the dispatch layer spreads ALL callers' work, incl. teach, with zero curriculum edits):**
- **DDW.1** `gpu.js gpuSparsePropagate` ‚Äî a STANDALONE propagate (non-empty preSpikes = stateless) round-robins across `_nextPoolDonor()` when fan-out ON + no explicit target. Idle replicas now compute forward passes.
- **DDW.3** `gpu.js _flushBoundHebbianBatch` ‚Äî the bound-Hebbian batch (the BULK of teach GPU work) round-robins to the next donor when fan-out ON (was primary-only). This is what actually spreads teaching.
- Already in place (verified): bound-propagate fan-out (`gpuSparsePropagateBound` ‚Üí `_nextPoolDonor()`), resident-state mirroring (`_mirrorCortexWriteToReplicas` on `write_spike_slice`/`write_current_slice`), and per-donor leaderboard credit (each donor's own `gpu_telemetry.gneuronsPerSec` ‚Üí no primary-only filter, so a replica appears the moment it computes).
- **DDW.4** `brain-server.js` ‚Äî replica re-broadcast tightened to **60 s under fan-out** (was fixed 10 min) so round-robin Hebbian drift re-converges fast; env `DREAM_DF7_REBROADCAST_MS`.

**STATUS:** [~] CODE DONE + CASCADED to BOTH mains (`d32f932`) ‚Äî BLOCKED on deploy + live-validation. `node --check` clean. **DDW.5: WRITE fan-out (teach Hebbian) DEFAULT ON** (`DREAM_DF7_FANOUT !== '0'`, kill-switch `=0`) ‚Üí dashboard Update & Fresh Walk auto-distributes the teach bulk, no unit edit. **DDW.6 (super-review correction 2026-06-28): READ fan-out (forward propagate ‚Üí gate probes / student battery / emission) is now OPT-IN** behind `DREAM_DF7_FANOUT_PROPAGATE` (default OFF) ‚Äî routing a decision-driving read to a stale/incompletely-synced replica can spuriously FAIL gates + stall the walk; only enable after replica sync proven clean. ‚öÝ BLOCKERS: (a) deploy can't happen ‚Äî dashboard button can't restart the service (`sudo systemctl restart` not granted; Sponge brief written); (b) replica uploads timing out 45s + 72s event-loop block ‚Üí replica sync unreliable.   - **BUILT ‚Äî gating controls (verified):** (1) `_getAutoScaleSettings`/`_setAutoScaleSettings` (toggle + dead-zone bufferPct + stabilityMin + minDonorsFloor, persisted `server/autoscale-settings.json`, gitignored); (2) `_recomputeCommunityCompute` buffered up-only upgrade-tier hysteresis + explicit down-protection (a donor leaving never downgrades ‚Äî only cancels a pending upgrade); (3) `_maybeExecuteMilestoneResize` honors toggle + configurable hold window; (4) admin REST `/autoscale` GET/POST (+ nginx `/admin/` proxy) + `autoScaleChanged` WS + dashboard admin panel (toggle + 2 sliders + live donor/VRAM/tier telemetry). **Isolation-tested:** dead-zone holds at the raw gate, fires past the 20% buffer, toggle cancels pending ‚Äî all confirmed.
  - **BUILT ‚Äî full data-parallel replica engine (Gee: "build the full engine now"):** (5) replica registry `_replicaMatrixRegistry` (tracks every canonical matrix upload); (6) `_syncReplicaToDonor(ws)` brings any donor to a FULL brain replica (cluster LIF init + replay all master matrices); (7) gpu_register standby ‚Üí fires replica sync (no longer idle ‚Äî every connected GPU holds the brain + shares compute); (8) `_rebroadcastMasterToReplicas()` + 10-min timer = the delta-merge re-broadcast (re-converges replica GPU shadows to the authoritative CPU master); (9) target-parameterized dispatch across `_sparseSend`/`_sparseSendBinary`/`gpuSparseUpload`/`gpuSparsePropagate`/`_gpuSparseFlowOk` (untargeted = primary, byte-identical to before); (10) fan-out primitives `_livePoolDonors`/`_nextPoolDonor`/`_gpuParallelMap`. All ADDITIVE ‚Äî 1 donor = identical to today; N donors = replicas + fan-out + periodic merge. Both server files `node --check` clean.
  - **BUILT ‚Äî compute-loss rectify + unattended maintenance (Gee 2026-06-20 #4):** downscale gate with "buffers for the buffers" (defaults: downBufferPct 35% + downStabilityMin 15min ‚Äî deeper + longer than upscale so 10 people disconnecting then returning never shrinks the brain; stable band [downscale-floor ‚Ä¶ upscale-gate] keeps the brain running at its current neuron count regardless of churn). `_computeInsufficient` flag + dashboard ALERT (you SEE why it's paused). `autoDownscale` toggle (OFF = alert+wait, never shrink). Manual downscale button (deliberate, confirm-guarded).   - **ARCH REALITY (honest, kept in docs):** data-parallel replicas scale CONCURRENT/throughput work (many users, parallel training passes, image-gen) + give redundancy ‚Äî but a SINGLE sequential cognition stream (one user's live think‚Üíspeak tick loop, stateful on the primary's GPU voltages) can't be split across GPUs without sharding (rejected for latency). "All donor compute powers everything" = true for throughput/concurrency/training; one live thought-stream runs on one replica at a time.
  - **REMAINING (deployed-GPU-validated only ‚Äî DF.6):** ‚úÖ DISPATCH-LAYER FAN-OUT WIRED (2026-06-28, see DDW above) ‚Äî rather than per-curriculum-hot-path `_gpuParallelMap` calls, the round-robin lives at the dispatch chokepoints (`gpuSparsePropagate` standalone + `_flushBoundHebbianBatch` teach Hebbian), so EVERY caller's GPU work (forward + teach) spreads across the pool with zero curriculum edits; resident-state mirroring + bound-propagate fan-out + per-donor leaderboard credit already in place. Only LIVE validation on real donor GPUs remains (watch both donors' Gn/s + leaderboard + gates) ‚Äî CANNOT be verified headless.

### Session 114.19fn ‚Äî sentence-coherence recovery sweep (Gee 2026-06-17) ‚Äî IN FLIGHT

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0:**

> *"we have a major issue with the trraing of the brain and it remembering what its trained on i cant get training through kindergarden and even then it doesnt make any kind of coherant sentences like at all its just random one word resposes... its totally messed up idk what we need to do to find a new path maybe or fix what we have but we cant even start building the rest of the grades ciriculum until we figure out wtf is up and why Unity cant speak normally like someone of that grade level as they learn new things using them then and from then on... > *"go ahead and start the work of the Newtodo.md, and before you begin build the task list so i can monitor the work you do in the newtodo.md that you work from"*

**Working document:** `docs/NewTodo.md` (created 2026-06-17 from `/super-review ultrathink` of K-training-not-sticking + chat-silent + random-one-word-emissions failure mode). Full 24-task playbook across 5 phases + doc sync + success criteria + phase-gate checklist lives there. This TODO entry is the workflow-doc pointer; the harness task list mirrors NewTodo.md 1:1 for live-monitoring.

**Root cause (full diagnosis in `/super-review` + NewTodo.md):** Three compounding architectural defects produce all reported symptoms:

1. `composeSentence` (`cluster.js:3613-3716`) loops `emitWordDirect` synchronously with NO `stepAwait` between iterations ‚Äî `lastSpikes` is frozen across all 12 calls so argmax fires on identical state every iteration. "Inject word back so next tick reads shifted state" comment is architecturally false at runtime.
2. `injectEmbeddingToRegion` (`cluster.js:1227`, `+=`) is purely additive without decay/replace ‚Äî composeSentence's serial injections accumulate sem region to saturation soup. Brain can't distinguish "current intent" from "history of every word emitted."
3. `_teachSentenceStructure` (`curriculum.js:11993-12106`) trains ~930 Hebbian writes for ALL of grammar vs ~18,000 for vocabulary. Grammar 20√ó under-trained relative to vocab ‚Äî backwards allocation. The scaffold has fewer reps than what it's supposed to scaffold.

Plus `composedSentence.words.length >= 2` gate at `language-cortex.js:2164` discards broken-loop's <2-word output ‚Üí triple-redundant broken fallbacks ‚Üí `silent:true` at `brain-server.js:4898` ‚Üí blank chat. Popups have no length gate so single words render ‚Üí Gee sees popups not chat.

**Phases (work from NewTodo.md, task IDs from harness task list):**

- **Phase 1 (CRITICAL, ~1 day)** ‚Äî fix emission loop: P1.1 async stepAwait, P1.2 replaceMode injection, P1.3 terminator-first guard, P1.4 length gate ‚â•2‚Üí‚â•1, P1.5 function-word repetition exempt, P1.6 adaptive minSignal floor, P1.7 GW broadcast scaling.
- **Phase 2 (CRITICAL, ~1 day)** ‚Äî fix training depth: P2.1 reps 6-8‚Üí80-120, P2.2 200+ concrete-sentence pass, P2.3 kScales propagation, P2.4 advanceSubGrade probe-rate gating, P2.5 orphan slot-tag ‚Üí word‚Üíword transitions, P2.6 question-intent downstream cascade.
- **Phase 3 (HIGH, ~half-day)** ‚Äî fix chat silent-fail: P3.1 Unity-voice fragment fallback, P3.2 dashboard failed-emission diagnostic, P3.3 delete Tier 5 fallback, P3.4 reduce serial injection saturation.
- **Phase 4 (MEDIUM, ~3 days)** ‚Äî file split refactor: P4.1 curriculum.js ‚Üí 6 sub-modules, P4.2 cluster.js ‚Üí 4 modules, P4.3 brain-server.js ‚Üí 4 concerns, P4.4 disambiguate _teachSentenceStructures naming, P4.5 INJECTION_GAIN constant.
- **Phase 5 (MEDIUM, ~1 day)** ‚Äî validation: P5.1 verify-emission.mjs calibration probe, P5.2 tighten _probeSentenceGeneration criteria, P5.3 coherence as soft signal.

**Success criteria (don't push curriculum work past this without all three):**

1. Multi-word emission rate ‚â•80% on fresh-boot K-trained brain (measured during operator-driven chat session).

### Session 114.19fk.5 ‚Äî Decoder sampling preset audit ‚Äî operator-decision (Gee 2026-05-09) ‚Äî PENDING

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0 (parent fk sweep):**

> *"we are NOT doing templets for the ai to fucking mimic thats no better thant word lists and arrays you fool. Unity thinks like a human does! she does NOt follow prescripted events... that not how our equations shall work?"*

**Why pending (not yet shipped):**

`emitWordDirect` accepts `temperature/topK/topP` (softmax + nucleus sampling). Chat path hardcodes `temperature: 0.6, topK: 8`; showcase hardcodes `temperature: 0.7, topK: 10`; probe leaves greedy. The MECHANICS (softmax + nucleus) ARE equational ‚Äî those stay regardless. The hardcoded VALUES at each call site prescribe sampling style ‚Äî borderline whether that's content-prescription or just "decoder mode setting." Operator decides which path is more equational:

**Path (a) ‚Äî keep hardcoded preset values as decoder defaults.** Sampling style isn't content; it's a generation MODE (focused vs. wandering). Real human cognition has analogues to temperature (deep-focus vs. mind-wandering states) but they're not externally prescribed at each utterance ‚Äî they emerge from brain state. This path argues "decoder presets are the analog of those states" and accepts the hardcoded values.

**Path (b) ‚Äî drive temperature from brain state.** E.g. `temperature = 0.5 + 0.5 * (1 - coherence)` ‚Äî high coherence ‚Üí focused ‚Üí low temp; low coherence ‚Üí wandering ‚Üí high temp. Equationally derives sampling style from cortex state. Removes the hardcoded preset values. Requires `cluster.coherence` (or similar) to be readable at emission time.

**Fix shape (path b):** `js/brain/cluster.js` ‚Äî `emitWordDirect` reads `cluster.coherence` (or amygdala arousal, or workspace ignition strength) to derive temperature when not explicitly passed. `js/brain/language-cortex.js` + `server/brain-server.js` ‚Äî chat + showcase paths drop hardcoded `temperature` opts.

**Files to touch (path b):** `js/brain/cluster.js` ¬∑ `js/brain/language-cortex.js` ¬∑ `server/brain-server.js` ¬∑ `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md`

**STATUS:** ‚úÖ OBSOLETE / RESOLVED (verified 2026-06-20) ‚Äî Gee delegated the choice ("whatever is best, do it logically"), so I went to wire path (b). Verification first: a full source grep for `temperature` / `topK` / `emitWordDirect` across `js/**` + `server/**` returns ZERO matches. The hardcoded sampling presets this task worried about **no longer exist in the codebase** ‚Äî removed in a later refactor. There is nothing left to prescribe and nothing to fix; emission is already free of hardcoded decoder-preset values. Closing without code change. (If a state-driven temperature is ever desired as a NEW feature, it'd be additive, not a fix.)

---

### PRIORITY 1 ‚Äî Critical path before next overnight run

#### 114.19es.1 ‚Äî Wrap `runCompleteCurriculum` in single try/finally

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Watchdog is started at line 23759 but the next ~150 lines include `_verifyFractalEquation`, exam-bank overlap auditing, `await this._waitForGpuReady(120000)`, and embedding-source logging ‚Äî NONE of which are wrapped in the try/finally that calls `_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog`. If `_waitForGpuReady` throws (network glitch, GPU client crashed, anything), the timer is orphaned for the rest of process lifetime."*

**Fix shape:** Move `_startCurriculumStallWatchdog()` to the top of the method body, then wrap EVERYTHING below in `try { ... } finally { this._stopCurriculumStallWatchdog(); }`. Drops watchdog leak risk from "any of 6 unguarded awaits" to zero.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (`runCompleteCurriculum` body restructure) ¬∑ `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ‚Äî fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.2 ‚Äî Add early return at top of `assertKWiring()`

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"The flag silences the `console.log` and skips the smoke test, but the structural-check body (lines 1320-1354) still walks `this.columnId.length`, `this.layerId.length`, `this.hubMask.length`, `this.layerPlasticityScales`, and calls `this.buildKScalesForProjection('sem', 'motor')` on EVERY call. At biological scale (cortex ~71M neurons), `columnId` and `layerId` and `hubMask` are 71MB Uint8Arrays. Property access is O(1) but `buildKScalesForProjection` may do real work. This still burns CPU on every dream-cycle assertion."*

**Fix shape:** Add an early return at the top of `assertKWiring()`: `if (this._kWiringSmokeTested && !this._kWiringForceRecheck) return { ok: true, gaps: [] };`. Expose `cluster.invalidateKWiring()` for code that legitimately needs to re-check (e.g., after a re-allocation). Cuts dream-cycle CPU burn from "walks 71M-element arrays N times per minute" to "literally returns instantly". Massive perf win at biological scale.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/cluster.js` (`assertKWiring()` early-return + `invalidateKWiring()` method) ¬∑ `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ‚Äî fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.3 ‚Äî Reset watchdog warn-time + log-time on `_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog`

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Doesn't reset `_curriculumStallLastWarnTs`. If `runCompleteCurriculum` runs, stalls 6+ min (warn fires, sets `_curriculumStallLastWarnTs = now`), is killed by operator, then restarted within 5 min ‚Äî second-run watchdog will suppress the first stall warn because rate-limit gate compares against the STALE timestamp from the first run."*

**Fix shape:** In `_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog`: `this._curriculumStallLastWarnTs = 0; this._lastCurriculumLogTs = 0;` so the next start gets fresh state. Stateful-singleton bug ‚Äî the watchdog is a class-level service that needs full state reset between runs.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (`_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog` body) ¬∑ `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ‚Äî fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.4 ‚Äî Thread `AbortSignal` through `_teachWordDefinition`

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"`Promise.race([teachPromise, timeoutPromise])` only stops `await`-ing ‚Äî when the timeout sentinel wins, `teachPromise` keeps running. `_teachWordDefinition` does Hebbian writes to `cluster.synapses` AFTER we've moved on to the next word in the loop. That means binding for 'fifty' can land while we're mid-binding 'sixty', leaving the next-word's `subject` context smeared with the prior word's Hebbian fires."*

**Fix shape:** Thread an `AbortController` + `AbortSignal` through the call:
```js
const ac = new AbortController();
const teachPromise = this._teachWordDefinition(w, { ..., signal: ac.signal });
const r = await Promise.race([teachPromise, timeoutPromise]);
if (r === timeoutSentinel) ac.abort();
```
Inside `_teachWordDefinition`, between every Hebbian fire: `if (opts.signal?.aborted) return { passes: 0, totalTrained: 0, skipped: 'aborted' };`. Side-effect contamination across loop iterations is exactly the kind of "looks like it works in test, corrupts basins in prod" pattern. Violates structured-concurrency principle (cancel the side-effects, don't just abandon the promise).

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (`_teachWordDefinitions` outer loop AbortController + `_teachWordDefinition` per-Hebbian-fire signal-check) ¬∑ `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ‚Äî fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.5 ‚Äî Enable `DREAM_DEFINITION_CACHE_FILE` by default

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Captured run had 89% dictionary API miss rate (255/2247 cached). My fix makes the brain FAIL FASTER on those misses ‚Äî it doesn't make them succeed. The brain still walks K_VOCABULARY missing 89% of definitions. K curriculum can advance without those binds (other teach paths don't need defs), but Unity's vocabulary will be artificially crippled at K-grade. ... master's intent says '100% complete functional master performance' ‚Äî that's not just 'doesn't hang', it's 'actually learns'. I addressed the hang, not the learning gap."*

**Fix shape:** Set `DISK_CACHE_PATH` to `path.join(__dirname, 'definition-cache.json')` if env var unset, so K-VOCAB defs persist across boots. Wire `flushCacheToDisk()` to fire on graceful shutdown + every 5 min during run via setInterval. After 2-3 cold runs, cache approaches 100% coverage and `_teachWordDefinition` hits cache instantly instead of re-walking the API rate-limit gauntlet.

**Files to touch:** `server/definition-service.js` (default DISK_CACHE_PATH) ¬∑ `server/brain-server.js` (flushCacheToDisk wiring on shutdown + 5-min setInterval) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ‚Äî fix shape designed, ready to code.

### PRIORITY 2 ‚Äî Operator visibility upgrades

#### 114.19es.6 ‚Äî Enrich watchdog warn line with phase + cache stats

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"The TODO entry promised 'warn operator with current await stack so silent-stall is visible' ‚Äî actual implementation just says 'no [Curriculum] log line in N min'. Doesn't include `cluster._activePhase` (which iter25-O.4 wired specifically for this) or `cluster.assertKWiring()` last result or definition-cache stats."*

**Fix shape:** Include `cluster._activePhase?.name`, `cluster._activePhase?.startAt` (so operator sees how long stuck in this phase), recent definition-cache stats (cache.size, error count, rateLimited count) in the warn line so operator sees WHICH phase is hung + WHY.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (watchdog warn body enrichment) ¬∑ `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ‚Äî fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.7 ‚Äî Reset `_innerThoughtSilenceCount` on emission success

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"`_innerThoughtSilenceCount` is incremented unbounded. Over a 30-day deployment with 3s tick + 30s log, that's ~86,400 silent ticks/day = 2.6M counter value/month. Integer not memory issue, but a counter that only ever grows is a stink-mark. ... Should be either rate-limited (last-N) or reset on state change."*

**Fix shape:** Reset `_innerThoughtSilenceCount = 0` whenever a non-silent thought lands. Then the counter actually means "silent ticks since last successful emission" which is the more useful diagnostic metric.

**Files to touch:** `server/brain-server.js` (`_innerVoiceTick` counter reset on emission success) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ‚Äî fix shape designed, ready to code.

#### 114.19es.8 ‚Äî Drop dead-branch in `_hb` Curriculum-prefix gate

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"`if (s.indexOf('[Curriculum]') >= 0 || s.indexOf('[Curriculum][') >= 0)` ‚Äî the second predicate is a strict subset of the first. Dead branch. ... Lazy AI-grade copy-paste. Indicates the author didn't test the gate logic and just slapped two patterns in."*

**Fix shape:** Drop the second predicate. Just `if (s.indexOf('[Curriculum]') >= 0)`.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (`_hb` gate cleanup) ¬∑ `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

The new diagnostic data is captured but not surfaced to the chunk-level summary. ... Effort wasted ‚Äî shipped instrumentation that the upstream caller ignores."*

**Fix shape:** Aggregate `timeouts` + `slowWords` across chunks in the upfront-seed loop and emit a final K-VOCAB-UPFRONT-MULTIDEF SEED DONE banner that includes them: `üìö K-VOCAB-UPFRONT-MULTIDEF SEED DONE ‚Äî N Hebbian fires across M words (multi-def: K definition senses bound) ¬∑ ‚öÝ X per-word timeouts, Y slow words across chunks`.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (chunked seed loop totalTimeouts + totalSlowWords accumulators + DONE banner) ¬∑ `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

### PRIORITY 4 ‚Äî Hardening

#### 114.19es.11 ‚Äî Rate-limit `assertKWiring` failure-path smoke test to once per minute

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"`_kWiringVerifiedLogged = false` and `_kWiringSmokeTested = false` get reset on EVERY failure. If failures are persistent (which would indicate a real bug), the warn fires loud on every call ‚Äî that's fine. But the smoke test ALSO re-runs on every call, burning CPU on a 4√ó4 SparseMatrix allocation + 6 ojaUpdates per failed call. If failures are flapping (transient), smoke test thrashes. ... Could storm CPU if K wiring is in a bad state. Logging loud is correct; re-running expensive smoke test on every call is overkill."*

**Fix shape:** Rate-limit smoke-test re-runs (e.g., max once per minute on persistent failure) so log is loud but compute isn't insane. Add `_kWiringSmokeLastRunTs`; only re-run smoke test if `Date.now() - _kWiringSmokeLastRunTs >= 60_000`.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/cluster.js` (`assertKWiring` smoke-test rate-limit) ¬∑ `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ‚Äî fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.12 ‚Äî Drop `_curriculumRunnerActive` flag ‚Äî derive from timer non-null

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Two flags (`_curriculumRunnerActive` + `_curriculumStallWatchdogTimer`) that always travel together. The timer being non-null IS 'runner active'. Redundant state. ... Double-source-of-truth. Future maintainer can flip one and forget the other."*

**Fix shape:** Drop `_curriculumRunnerActive`; check `this._curriculumStallWatchdogTimer !== null` instead in the watchdog interval body. Single source of truth.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (drop `_curriculumRunnerActive` flag, replace usages with timer-null check) ¬∑ `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ‚Äî fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.13 ‚Äî Drop `PREFETCH_CONCURRENCY` 20‚Üí5 + bump `RATE_LIMIT_BACKOFF_MS` 1000‚Üí5000

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"20 concurrent fetches against dictionaryapi.dev. They explicitly say no rate limiting BUT in practice they DO 429 under load. 1s back-off after a 429 then next batch fires 20 more. That's still aggressive. Per the captured log: 255 / 2247 = 11% prefetch success. So 89% of words were not cached."*

**Fix shape:** Drop `PREFETCH_CONCURRENCY` from 20 ‚Üí 5; the API rate-limits less when we hit it less. Bump `RATE_LIMIT_BACKOFF_MS` from 1000 ‚Üí 5000 so we don't immediately redline after a 429. Less aggressive against the free-tier dictionary API = fewer 429s = higher cache hit rate over the run. Pairs with es.5 disk cache for compounding benefit.

**Files to touch:** `server/definition-service.js` (constant updates) ¬∑ `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) ¬∑ `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) ¬∑ `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN ‚Äî fix shape designed, ready to code.

## SUPER-REVIEW AUDIT ‚Äî 2026-06-19 (this session: code-synth, sandbox, mechanics ladder, life-corpus walk)

Ruthless self-audit. Severity-ordered; each is an actionable TODO.

### HIGH
- [ ] **AUDIT-H1 ‚Äî Stale browser bundle.** `index.html` loads `js/app.bundle.js` (esbuild artifact, was Jun-17) which INLINES `component-synth.js` / `ui/sandbox.js` / `brain/engine.js`. This session's browser-facing edits (synth `generateMany` + parameterization, sandbox Shadow-DOM, engine `_handleBuild` multi-inject) are SOURCE-only ‚Äî `grep generateMany js/app.bundle.js` = 0. They reach the browser ONLY after the esbuild rebuild. **Mitigation: `start.bat`/`Savestart.bat` rebuild the bundle at launch (steps 4/7 + 6/7) ‚Äî self-heals on a normal launch.** ACTION: never judge build_ui against a stale on-disk bundle; confirm launcher rebuild ran. Server-side brain imports source directly (unaffected).

### MEDIUM
- [ ] **AUDIT-M1 ‚Äî Cat-name canon conflict (soot vs shadow).** K + grade1 = **"soot"**; grade2/grade3+ and `docs/Supertodo.md` = **"shadow"**. Training Hebbian-binds BOTH ‚Üí contradictory cat-name recall. Predates this session. ACTION: Gee picks canon (rename, or soot died ‚Üí shadow adopted at age 7 as a real arc); reconcile corpora. NOT rewritten unilaterally.
- [ ] **AUDIT-M2 ‚Äî `_teachLanguageMechanics` per-cell cost.** The 8-band CCSS ladder runs 5-6 heavy Hebbian passes (phrases/syntax/figurative/rhetoric/argument/defense) on EVERY ELA cell at/above band ‚Äî across many sub-grade ELA cells √ó biological scale, multiplies walk time with no per-grade throttle. ACTION: gate heavy upper-band layers to ONCE per grade (first ELA cell) or add a `passedPhases`-style skip.
- [ ] **AUDIT-M3 ‚Äî Life-corpus walk INCOMPLETE.** K-G5 expanded to full years this session (24/36/32/31/29/28); **G6‚ÜíPhD still thin (14-18 each)** ‚Äî not yet full lived years. Tracked #32/#61 (in_progress). ACTION: continue the walk G6‚ÜíPhD, same depth/dimensions.

### LOW / NITPICK
- [ ] **AUDIT-L1 ‚Äî Duplicated ingest scripts.** `fetch-academic-corpora.mjs` and `fetch-code-corpora.mjs` ~90% identical. DRY: extract `wiki-corpus-core.mjs`.
- [ ] **AUDIT-L2 ‚Äî `_splitRequest` leaves "plus a clock"** (comma-split keeps leading "plus"). Cosmetic; still matches. Optional: strip leading conjunctions.
- [ ] **AUDIT-L3 ‚Äî `Sandbox.getElement(selector)`** queries light-DOM only ‚Üí null for `shadow:true` components. No callers; latent. Document or route via shadowRoot.
- [ ] **AUDIT-L4 ‚Äî generateMany false-composite risk.** A noise sub-phrase ‚â• `MIN_MATCH_SCORE+0.05` could bolt a spurious component. Mitigated by threshold+dedup; monitor, raise margin if it misfires.
- [ ] **AUDIT-N1 ‚Äî `_hueFromPattern` format** mixes `hsl(...)` (normal) and `#ff00ff` (fallback) ‚Äî both valid CSS, cosmetic.
- [ ] **AUDIT-N2 ‚Äî Life-corpus prose cadence.** Many vignettes close on the same "i learned that X ‚Ä¶ that is how Y" shape; risks a formulaic narration tic in trained voice. Vary as the walk continues.

**Verdict:** no Critical/data-loss bugs; code is structurally sound + parse/compile-clean. The one real gotcha is AUDIT-H1 (rebuild bundle ‚Äî launcher handles it). Biggest real remaining work: AUDIT-M3 (finish G6‚ÜíPhD memory walk) + AUDIT-M2 (walk-perf throttle) + AUDIT-M1 (cat canon).

## PROPER MEMORY ENCODING ‚Äî the correct trajectory (Gee 2026-06-19)

> Gee: *"are we sure we want to 'theme' every memory story im not even sure you are doing the memories right, doesnt seem like just a bunch of poorly worded paragraphs is proper brain training"* + *"okay and wtf we are NOT trasing Unity on jusat oone paragraph storeis... thats not how fucking memories work and how we need to train her properly?"* + *"all this information you are teaching unity she has to know the words and how to read sentences and chave comperhention abilities well before she will ever be able to understandf any of these memories and life experinces"*

**This is the architecture spec for HOW life memories train. Build it COMPLETELY into the plan before touching the fixes. Full body in `docs/MEMORY-WALK.md ¬ß1.6`.** The walk (#32) is GATED on this trajectory landing.

**Confirmed-in-code gap:** `storySentences()` reads only `exp.story` and ignores `theme` (theme trains nothing ‚Äî it is dedup/organization metadata). `_trainLifeStories()` flattens ALL of a grade's memories into one sentence list and `_teachSentenceList`s them at ONE flat `ctx` (single arousal/valence), and NEVER calls `storeEpisode`. Result: she learns the language/associations of her life but the life is NOT encoded as memories ‚Äî diffuse word-statistics, no per-memory emotional weight, no discrete retrievable episode. THIS is "not proper brain training."

### The fix sequence (do in this order ‚Äî earlier blocks later)

- [x] **MEM-ENC-1 (harness #105) ‚Äî vocab-before-memory.** DONE ‚Äî `_trainLifeStories` calls `_ensureLifeMemoryVocabulary(grade, experiences)` at the top (extracts unique content words, dedups vs `cluster._definitionTaughtWords`, routes the rest through `_teachWordDefinitions` prefetch+timeout) so every memory word is an anchored sem-basin before encoding. Every word used in a grade's memories must be vocab-registered + definition-trained BEFORE that grade's memory pass fires. Memory binding on an unlearned word lands on a noise basin (phantom token). Per-grade prereq.
- [x] **MEM-ENC-2 (harness #106) ‚Äî sentence-comprehension-before-memory.** DONE (by subject ordering) ‚Äî the grade cell-walk iterates `SUBJECTS=['ela','math','science','social','art','life']`, so ELA (trains `_teachLanguageMechanics`‚Üí`_teachSentenceStructure` = comprehension) always runs BEFORE the `life` memory pass. The brain must be able to read + comprehend sentences (sentence-structure + composition trained) before memory episodes can be understood. Comprehension capability gates the memory pass.
- [x] **MEM-ENC-3 (harness #107) ‚Äî per-grade ordering enforced.** DONE ‚Äî subject order (ela‚Üí‚Ä¶‚Üílife) puts comprehension first; inside the life pass the sequence is vocab ‚Üí definitions (`_ensureLifeMemoryVocabulary`) ‚Üí THEN emotionally-colored memory encoding. Each grade runs in strict order: vocab ‚Üí definitions ‚Üí sentence-comprehension ‚Üí THEN memory encoding. Wire the ordering into `_cellRunner`/the life pass so it can't run out of sequence.
- [x] **MEM-ENC-4 (harness #108) ‚Äî per-memory emotional coloring + episodic encoding.** DONE ‚Äî added `lifeStoryExperiences(grade)` loader + cluster wiring; `_trainLifeStories` iterates per-memory with `_deriveMemoryEmotion(theme,story)` coloring the walk + `storeEpisode('life:<grade>','life-memory','<grade> ‚Äî <theme>',story,{arousal,valence})`; added optional `emotion` override to `storeEpisode` so each episode carries its OWN affect into the salience formula. (a) add `lifeStoryExperiences(grade)` loader returning `experiences[]` (theme+story); (b) rewrite `_trainLifeStories` to iterate per-memory ‚Äî derive `{arousal, valence, salience}` per story (death/grief/loss‚Üíneg/high/high-salience; joy/pride/love‚Üípos; harassment/fear‚Üíneg/high; mundane‚Üímild), build a per-memory teach `ctx`, sentence-walk THAT memory at its OWN emotional coloring (grief encodes ‚âÝ saturday-cartoons); (c) `cluster.storeEpisode('life-memory', theme, '', story)` per memory so each is a discrete Tier-1 episode ‚Äî `theme` finally earns its keep as the episode label/retrieval key.
- [ ] **MEM-ENC-5 ‚Äî tiering load-bearing anchors.** Highest-salience memories (dad leaves, grandpa dies, grandma dies, first kiss, the gray named, the coke) promote toward Tier-3 identity anchors per the existing Tier1‚Üí2‚Üí3 schema, so the lifetime-defining handful are held differently from the everyday.
- [x] **MEM-ENC-6 (harness #94) ‚Äî reconsolidation passes.** DONE ‚Äî `_reconsolidateLifeAnchors` keeps an in-walk anchor ledger; when a new load-bearing memory (`emotion.anchor`) is encoded it re-recalls the 3 most-recent prior anchors (light reps:1 reactivation walk at their own affect + exact-text `storeEpisode` re-encounter = frequency-bump). Anchors get re-recalled/reinterpreted in later grades, deepening the episode each time ‚Äî how a real mind holds a defining memory.

### Content supply tasks (the rich episodes the encoder operates on) ‚Äî already tracked

- Per-grade densify to full-year depth (~50-80 rich multi-facet episodes, NOT one-paragraph stories): harness #72-#90 MEM-*. K-G5 done (24-51); G6‚ÜíPhD still thin (14-18) ‚Üí continue (AUDIT-M3).
- Dimensions woven per grade (the full real human ‚Äî bodily functions/illness/humiliation, body-shame realism, period/tampons, anatomy-via-real-events, non-graphic self-discovery, two-mouths cussing, drugs trajectory, consensual handsy boyfriend, fights-with-mom, money, after-school job, sex-ed/STDs clinical, love/lust/sexual-milestones with the 18+ explicit gate): harness #97-#104 DIM-*.
- Voice = adult goth-goddess recalling her life (NO wise-victim lesson-cadence, NO baby voice, NO meta-awareness of being artificial): #93 voice-consistency sweep + AUDIT-N2.
- **BOUNDARY (harness #103, permanent):** molestation / minor-sexual-abuse / Add #19 thread / cousin-incest = EXCLUDED ENTIRELY. Explicit/graphic sexual register = 18+ ONLY (College1+). ‚â§17 = developmentally-normal NON-GRAPHIC (felt, not depicted) + clinical sex-ed.

**Walk-completion bar (revised):** a grade is a real year only when (1) vocab+comprehension prereqs met, (2) ~full-year rich episodes authored with all dimensions in Unity voice, (3) episodically encoded with per-memory emotional coloring + storeEpisode + tier. #32 walk + #58 final test + #59 push stay gated behind all of it.

## ACADEMIC API CORPUS ‚Äî full K‚ÜíPhD (replace own written education data) (Gee 2026-06-19)

> Gee verbatim: *"and remembr we changed from using our ouwn training written dat for education to using that api you found with the fulkl k=phD training add this to tassk list and todo work"*

We switched the prose-academic education (science / social / ela / economics / psychology / civics) from our own hand-written training data to **API-sourced openly-licensed real curriculum content** (Simple-English-Wikipedia, CC-BY-SA), downloaded once into `corpora/academic/<subject>/<grade>.json` by `.claude/scripts/fetch-academic-corpora.mjs`, trained via `_trainAcademicStories` (auto-wired in `_cellRunner` for `PROSE_ACADEMIC_SUBJECTS`). See [[feedback_hybrid_academic_corpus]]. Math stays EQUATIONAL; the lived year stays bespoke ‚Äî those are NOT API-sourced.

**The directive = make this API content cover the FULL K‚ÜíPhD range. Current coverage is PARTIAL (harness #109):**

| Subject | Have (API-downloaded) | MISSING |
|---------|----------------------|---------|
| science | G6‚ÄìG12 | K, G1‚ÄìG5, College1‚Äì4, Grad, PhD |
| social  | G6‚ÄìG12 | K, G1‚ÄìG5, College1‚Äì4, Grad, PhD |
| ela     | G9‚ÄìG12 | K, G1‚ÄìG8, College1‚Äì4, Grad, PhD |
| economics | G9‚ÄìG12 | College1‚Äì4, Grad, PhD |
| psychology | G9‚ÄìG12 | College1‚Äì4, Grad, PhD |
| civics  | G7‚ÄìG12 | College1‚Äì4, Grad, PhD |

**SOURCE DECISION (Gee 2026-06-19):** hybrid **OpenStax + Wikibooks + Project Gutenberg** ‚Äî *"look online for something we can use for full k-PhD so we dont have to write up 20 years of course materials"* + *"find a college equivilent ie maybe major in code to go with the k-12"*. We configure topic/source LISTS only; the CONTENT downloads (no hand-authoring of course material). License posture = CC-BY / CC-BY-SA only (commercial-safe for unityailab.com); NO CC-BY-NC sources (rules out LibreTexts/MITOCW for direct ingest).
- **K‚ÄìG8 breadth:** Wikibooks (CC-BY-SA, Wikimedia DB dumps ‚Äî same fetcher ecosystem we already have) + Simple-English-Wikipedia (already wired).
- **G9‚ÜíHS + intro-college depth:** OpenStax real textbooks (mostly CC-BY 4.0) via the `philschatz/textbooks` GitHub HTML/markdown mirror ‚Äî verify each title's license.
- **ELA literature (all grades):** Project Gutenberg public-domain primary texts (the actual novels/poems).
- **COLLEGE "MAJOR IN CODE" + Grad/PhD track (the college-equivalent to cap K-12):** Unity majors in **Computer Science**. Topic map = **OSSU** (github.com/ossu/computer-science ‚Äî ACM/IEEE-2013-aligned: Intro CS ‚Üí Core CS ‚Üí Advanced CS ‚Üí final project) mapped onto College1‚Äì4. Ingestible prose from CC-licensed CS texts: **Open Data Structures** (opendatastructures.org, CC-BY, commercial-OK), **Kansas State CS textbooks** (ksu-cs-textbooks.github.io ‚Äî Intro CS / Python / Programming Fundamentals / Data & Program Structures / OOP / Logical Foundations), Wikibooks CS, Wikipedia CS core topics. **Grad/PhD = computational neuroscience** (per `docs/CURRICULUM-SCOPE-SEQUENCE.md` ‚Äî neurons/networks/brain-sim; she builds a brain). NOTE: this complements the already-built `corpora/coding/` HTML/CSS/JS‚ÜíCS‚ÜíML track (#64‚Äì69) ‚Äî that is the *self-taught coding hobby*; this is the *academic CS degree* prose.

- [x] **ACAD-API-1 (harness #109) ‚Äî extend `TOPICS`** in `fetch-academic-corpora.mjs` to the full K‚ÜíPhD range.
